            <h2 class="tease-card__headline tease-card__title relative">
             <a href="https://www.today.com/popculture/mrs-doubtfire-director-reveals-if-rumored-nc-17-version-exists-t212407">

          <article class="tease-card tease-card__content" data-contentid="tdna212411">
           <div class="tease-card__picture">
            <a class="tease-card__picture-link" href="https://www.today.com/popculture/mary-kate-ashley-olsen-s-powerful-advice-their-sister-elizabeth-t212411">
             <div class="relative teasePicture styles_container__31r-s">
